There is no \\"perfect preservative\\" and we wish we didn't have to use a preservative at all, but the mold, bacteria, etc. preservatives kill are potentially far worse than preservatives. There aren't any preservatives that we like because the more effective they are, the less we like them for the body (the worst being parabens). So we had to go with the happy balance of it being proven to be the most effective while being shown to be safe.<br /><br />But, Geogard Ultra was found to be quite safe and is allowed to be used in natural and organic products. EWG.org rates it as a very low risk and most studies that show it as a risk are more talking about ingesting rather than applying to the skin. Plus, there are very low levels in our products.<br /><br />I have also seen the study on Vitamin C and Sodium Benzoate. Like any chemical reaction, this reaction requires certain conditions. This particular reaction is very sensitive. In order for this reaction to move at a noticeable rate, it needs heat and oxygen, in the absence of sugars and many common cosmetic ingredients. Cosmetic products just don't provide the proper condition for benzene formation.<br /><br />Here's an excerpt from the study \\"In fact extremely large amounts of Sodium Benzoate would need to be ingested in order to produce even slight toxic consequences for the body. In studies where mice have been fed a substantial diet of sodium benzoate, the data clearly indicate that their life expectancies were not shortened, nor was any notable health affect present at all.\\"<br /><br />Further, side effects associated with excess sodium benzoate are only linked to HUGE consumption internally in foods.<br /><br />For our formulation it is very safe, being a low PH acidic formula.<br /><br />But I want all customers to be 100% happy so if you have any doubts about using it, just let me know and I'm happy to issue a full refund. It's rich and silky, has a soft natural cocoa smell that dissipates, and is so nice and thick that you feel like you'll never have to put on lotion again. Except you do. Like, 30 minutes later when you feel your hands starting to crackle again. Nextly, I like to put it on my face post-washing, and this produces an.... odd effect. Namely, beads of perspiration take over my face for about 15 minutes, or until it sinks in I suppose. My theory is that the thickness I spoke of earlier starts to suffocate my pores and they try to break free be producing geysers of sweat. That's science.<br /><br />And one last thing: there are waaaaaay to many ingredients, many of which I can't pronounce. Isn't that like, Twinkie territory, and not organic face cream territory? Anyhow, I basically still want to buy it again because, you know, I like the way it makes me feel. Don't judge.
  399. Best product I've purchased for my skin this year.
